 patr likhane ke baad piemo ke aadesh par chaatra ko 1
 a loan of Rs 5 lakh has been received
 darasal, sara ne bank seajucation lonmanga tha lekin pichhlaa lone chuktaa naa karne kii vajah se lone nahin mil paaya

 haalanki yah lone duusare bank se mila he
 i was confident that PM would respond but did not expect it to be so fast, i got a reply in just 10 days: Sara, girl who wrote to PM # Karnatakapic
 twitter
 com / 5wkbvwfx3v — ANI (@ani_news) March 23, 2017 Sara High daughter, daughter of Abdul Ilyas of Mandya, Karnataka, wanted to pursue education, but was forced to take a loan from the bank due to lack of economic conditions
